First of all, in terms of price. On the Zhujun APP. The price here should definitely not be low. It also belongs to the charging standards of local first-class hotels.

Then, I will judge this place by the level of a first-class hotel. After all, as a consumer paying such a high amount of money, he must enjoy corresponding services and corresponding hardware facilities. This is the most basic right of consumers.

First of all, there is no "doorman" in the hotel. No one will pull the door to pick up your luggage when you get off the bus. This is the first point, my question here.

The second point is that it exists as a first-class fee. My mobile phone is Apple 12 Pro X. It cannot be charged while charging. personal assumptions. The plug is loose.

Second, the water pressure of the hotel's shower faucet is very low. The current is very small. The room I live in, 0523, also has a very slow water heating.

Second, as a charging first-class existence. The desk lamp didn't work when I first stayed in the hotel. As a worker who needs to work, this has a great impact on personal work. Later, I asked the staff to come up and replaced a light to make it easier to use.

Second, take my room 0523 as an example. Tap water has obvious microbes floating around that can be seen with the naked eye. And with a distinct smell. personal assumptions. It should belong to the long-term unprotected water pipes. lead to microbial growth. Of course, hotels seem to have their own interpretations.
